<Text>My family has been taking our pets (about 2 dozen feral and non-feral cats and one dog) to this location for nearly 20 years, obviously we are quite happy with them especially since it is a 30 minute drive to get there and you have to WANT to go when there are so many other choices that are closer.
We have have honest conversations with all the on-duty vets over years that run the gamut from the pros and cons of dental work, to the real hard choices facing us when it's time to make THE choice. We've never felt judged for making a non obvious choice, and always felt we were getting all the information we needed to make the right decision for us and our pets.
The office is compact, you walk in directly to the waiting area, with a check-in desk right there.
The 3 exam rooms are adjacent to the waiting area,  so no long walks in a maze of doors... it's all right there. The exam rooms have always been clean and organized. They do perform simple surgeries on site and euthanasias too.
Tips-
The waiting area is compact with about 10 individual chairs for all people waiting, so at busy times you may be close to another patron with their pet, so bring a cage or other method of keeping your pet close and out of bite or scratch range of other less pets.
If you have a favorite vet you want your pet to be seen by, you can call when you make the appointment and ask to be seen by that vet, be prepared to be flexible with your appointment date and time and make the appointment as early as possible.
Parking is right out front, there is usually an open spot close to the office, if not there are plenty of other spaces just a few feet further away.
There is a donut shop next door for the longer waits.</Text></record>

< Review>
Hal's Auto Care went above and beyond for me recently.  I had multiple service maintenance items performed on my Honda Accord recently.  However, when picking up my car, there was a serious problem.  The engine sounded horrible.  They offered a loaner vehicle and took it back in the shop.  They spent the next few days troubleshooting what might have gone wrong.  Methodically, they began to rule out their work as they analyzed the car.  They even called my previous Honda dealer where I got my car serviced to try to identify the problem.  After about a week they found the problem to be the timing belt had jumped 5 teeth on the rea cam.  It turned out to be a failed hydraulic tensioner.  The thing is, they didn't do any work on that or anything related so it was unlikely to be due to their fault.  But because it happened on their lot they took ownership of the issue.  They ended up fixing it and working out a very reasonable deal.  They also did not charge me for all the diagnosis time for troubleshooting.  This was a very unfortunate coincidence that they took ownership of and it really proved how great they are.  Their team is humble and trust worthy.  I highly recommend them.</Review>

**If you're going to take the time to read my post/review, please be kind enough to hit LIKE**
Let my start off by saying that my family & I love this place! Do√±a Maria's Pupusas are amazing! This place has some of the best Pupusas & in a variety of options. Hard to just pick a few. On our latest visit we had a spread of dishes. We hadn't been to this establishment in awhile & couldn't decide what we wanted so we had everything we'd craved prior to our visit. This restaurant is a quaint, clean & wholesome location. The family that runs it is always so nice & welcoming. They not only offer some of the finest quality in their food but also offer a array of foods. But the reason we were there was for authentic Salvadoran food! Pupusas (variety), platano frito con frojoles, tamal de pollo, empanadas de platano rellenas de frijol o crema. 1 of my kids had a cocktel de camaron & another had an asada burrito. I mean, we had an unbelievable table spread! We sat there & ate most of it. The drinks! I was there & couldn't think of anything else but their Fresco de Ensalada(natural fruit water drink) because I wanted the full Salvadoran dinning experience & it was amazing! The prices for our outstanding dinning experience was phenomenal! Very affordable & that's for a family of 4, myself & my 3 kids. If you're looking for some good, down to earth authentic Salvadoran food without being disappointed thorn I highly recommend you visit Do√±a Maria's. You'll enjoy it!<//review>

The atmosphere, service, and bocce ball were all great and made for a fun night. The food was simply alright. Generally, I found the food to be under-salted and under-seasoned. The goat cheese bruschetta was a nice appetizer, but the fried ravioli tasted bland by comparison (and came with a tragically sized side of marinara). The family-style entrees were palatable but quite forgettable for the most part.< /Review>

< Review>
We tend to come out to bocce ball two to three times a year as it is a favorite of some of us in the corporate world when guests come to town or we want and activity outing. Bocce ball is great because it is accessible to all skill levels and ages. That's not to say that you will be great at it but everyone can pick it up in a very short amount of time. Campo di bocce is the go-to place, and frankly, I'm not sure who or where or what the competition would be as the only other bocce ball place I am aware of without doing any research is the Campo di bocce in Fremont. But this being the original, they have got it down. from the time you arrive and waiting for your court time you can fill your experiments with a beer or wine. Be forewarned however, that they do not serve mixed drinks and that beer and wine are going to be your only options for an alcoholic experience. Once your court time has arrived your group will he gathered for a quick rundown and rules and when the game starts you can have drinks and food to accompany your activity which is one of the greatest experiences Campo di bocce offers with competition drinks and eats being a hard combination to beat. When I Court time was over we were seated at the tables for a dinner which was served buffet-style and included penne pasta with sausage, beef in a mushroom sauce with mushrooms, it seemed to be a light angel hair pasta, chicken, and a caesar salad. Bread and butter was also offered. All of the food was surprisingly good as I find that buffet food is hard to retain good flavor when made in large quantities. After everyone was done eating the staff was kind enough to give us to go boxes to take home any of the leftovers.whatever kind of night you are planning for a small or large group I am sure that Campo di bocce will take really good care of you and I highly recommend this establishment for the activity the food and the experience.< /Review>

< review>
Food pretty much sucks. It's what you'd expect of suburban Italian -- overly complex, trying too hard to be foodie, ultimately inauthentic. If you have special dietary needs, this menu will annoy you. The bocce area is filled with drunk bros desperately trying to compete for an alpha dog position, unsupervised children running loose across the boards, and (on the two trips I've been forced to endure here) a disheartening population of lonely singles looking for some connection, but finding only the harrowing collisions of cupid's bocce balls against their hearts. I sometimes think it would be merciful to shut this building down, for it must often weep. Beer is okay, though, and parking is plentiful.<//review>
